Ahem. Getting a bit carried away there. The point is, I had grand visions of Max with a modern, sexy ’do that would perfectly complement his new designer getups. So I booked us an appointment at the hippest salon in town and practically dragged my protesting boyfriend through the doors.

“I like my hair the way it is, Pen,” he tried to reason as we settled into the waiting area. “It’s low-maintenance, you know?”

“Psh, where’s the fun in that?” I scoffed, thumbing through a stack of hairstyle magazines. “With just a little product and a daring new cut, we’ll have your luscious locks turning heads all over town!”

Mr. Snuffles snickered at that, mumbling something about turning Max’s head into a “glorified toilet brush.” But I was too preoccupied studying photos of debonair gentlemen with expertly quaffed coifs to pay him any mind.

When our stylist finally called us back, I presented her with my grand vision…and that’s where everything went terribly, horribly awry.

“So, you’re envisioning something along the lines of a textured pompadour? Maybe with some long, face-framing layers for movement?” she asked, deftly running a comb through Max’s shaggy mane.

“Exactly!” I exclaimed, clapping my hands together. “A little bit of roguish charm, a touch of modern sophistication. Just think ‘James Dean meets Ryan Gosling’ and you’ve got the general vibe.”

Famous last words, my friends. Because two hours later, Max emerged from that salon chair looking like…well, like a bedraggled, overgrown poodle.

“Oh. My. Doggy bags,” I gasped, hands flying to my mouth as he shuffled out with his head hanging low. “Maxwell Rover, what in the breed name did they do to you?!”

The stylist had taken my vague instructions for “messy yet stylish” and run wild, leaving Max with an unfortunate hybrid of a mullet and a full-body shave. The top was a wild tangle of choppy layers that stuck out in frazzled tufts, while the sides were practically sheared down to the skin. My boyfriend looked like a sheepdog that had gotten into a nasty fight with a lawnmower!

“I tried to warn you, Penelope,” Mr. Snuffles tutted, sauntering over to inspect the damage. “But noooo, you just had to go sticking your well-meaning snout where it didn’t belong. Now your poor boyfriend looks like a reject from the Crufts Dog Show.”

Ignoring his snide remarks (though I had to admit they stung with brutal accuracy), I turned to Max with the most apologetic expression I could muster.

“Oh sweetheart, I am so, so sorry,” I cooed, gently petting his threadbare head. “This is…well, it’s certainly a look, that’s for sure! But don’t worry, we’ll get it fixed. I promise.”

Max simply sighed and gave me a weary smile, his eyes silently pleading for this makeover madness to be over.

Step 3) The Skincare Snafu

You’d think after the haircut debacle, I would have learned my lesson about pushing my beautification agenda too far. But folks, when you’re a determined dogmama like me, you don’t just roll over and play dead at the first sign of chaos! No, you shake it off, re-fluff your fur, and forge ahead with that same boundless enthusiasm.

Which is precisely what I did as soon as Max’s traumatized tresses had grown out enough to be presentable again. This time, I decided to take a more…subtle approach to enhancing his natural assets. A skincare routine was just the ticket – a few targeted products to bring out his inner glow and have him looking refreshed, revitalized, and ready to take on the world!

“You cannot be serious,” Mr. Snuffles deadpanned when I unveiled my latest scheme over breakfast one morning. “First the clothes, then that haircut atrocity, and now you want to douse the poor sap in overpriced face gunk?”

I simply waved off his cynicism with a breezy trill. “Don’t be so dramatic, Snuffles! A little gentle exfoliation and some light moisturizing is hardly going to do Max any harm. In fact, I’ll bet he’ll love how smooth and radiant his skin feels afterwards!”

Max, bless his easygoing heart, just shrugged and smiled at me over his coffee mug. “If it makes you happy, babe, I’m game to try it.”

Famous last words, am I right? Because oh boy, did that skincare experiment go haywire in a hurry!

Our first attempt at a full facial regimen started out innocently enough. I laid out all my top-of-the-line products with the precision of a professional dog groomer – a luxurious cream cleanser, a gentle exfoliating scrub, a nutrient-rich mud mask, and a silky moisturizer to lock in all that hydrated goodness.

“Okay Max, just sit back and relax while I work my magic,” I instructed, rubbing my hands together in eager anticipation. “This is going to make your skin glow like a freshly-polished trophy!”

Max obediently closed his eyes as I slathered on the first layer of cleanser, gently massaging the creamy lather into his cheeks and forehead. So far, so good! That is, until I moved on to the exfoliating scrub…

“Gah! Pen, what is this stuff?” Max yelped, eyes flying open as the granular mixture made contact with his tender skin. “It feels like I’ve got a cheese grater being rubbed all over my face!”

I tried to sooth him, assuring him that a little gentle buffing was key to sloughing off dead skin cells and achieving that coveted radiance. But Max would have none of it, frantically pawing at his face in an attempt to wipe away the scratchy serum.

Before I knew it, there were flecks of scrub flung in every direction – coating the bathroom counter, speckling the mirror, and even catching me square in the eye at one point. Mr. Snuffles wisely retreated to a safe vantage point atop the toilet tank, watching the chaos unfold with a bemused shake of his fuzzy head.

“Seriously, Pen? You’re going to douse him in goop and expect him to just sit there and take it?” the snarky pup chided as Max bolted from the room, his entire face tinged an angry pink from the vigorous scrubbing. “He’s a boyfriend, not a poodle at the groomer’s.”

I’ll admit, at that moment my confidence wavered a bit. But I wasn’t about to let one minor skincare skirmish derail the entire operation! So after giving Max some space to recover (and maybe indulging in a consolation snack or two), I decided to switch tactics.

Rather than go for a full-on spa treatment, I’d start slow and ease him into a simplified routine, one gentle product at a time. A basic moisturizer was the perfect gateway – just a pea-sized amount to hydrate and rejuvenate his handsome mug. No harsh scrubs, no overpowering scents, just a straightforward cream to nourish and soften.

I should have known that even this stripped-down regimen wouldn’t go smoothly.

The first few nights were…well, let’s just say Max wasn’t quite accustomed to my nightly moisturizing ritual. More than once, I found myself chasing him around the apartment, moisturizer bottle in hand, pleading with him to let me work my magic.

“Max, honey, where are you? It’s time for your hydrating treatment!” I’d coo, squeezing out a dollop of the rich, fragrant cream. “This is going to make your skin feel like pure velvet, I promise!”

His muffled response usually came from whatever closet or cabinet he’d tucked himself into that day.

“No way, Pen! I’m not falling for your beauty trap again. You’ll just try to smother me in another one of your smelly face potions!”

Meanwhile, Mr. Snuffles would be parked on the couch, gleefully watching the chase unfold as I scurried from room to room in pursuit of my moisturizer-averse mate.

“I give it five minutes before he’s barricaded himself in the bathroom and you’re begging him to come out,” he’d taunt between bites of his chewy treat. “You know, for a ‘dog trainer,’ you sure are terrible at reading body language.”

Eventually, I’d manage to corner Max and quickly dab on a thin veil of moisturizer before he could wriggle free and disappear into another hidey-hole. All the while, I’d keep up a soothing stream of praise and encouragement, like I was calming a skittish puppy.

“There now, that’s not so bad, is it?” I’d croon, gently smoothing the cream along the apples of his cheeks. “You’re going to have the most lusciously hydrated skin on the block, my little stubble muffin!”

Max would just sigh and shake his head at me, resigning himself to being my perpetual makeover project. But hey, at least his complexion was looking more radiant by the day!

The Takeaway: Embrace the Flaws, Warts and All

So in the end, did Operation Dapper Boyfriend turn out to be the glamorous transformation I’d envisioned? Well…not quite. Despite my best efforts (and the occasional grooming-induced meltdown), Max emerged from this experience more or less the same lovably low-maintenance guy I’d fallen for in the first place.

Sure, his closet was a bit more stocked with fashion-forward apparel (most of which remained firmly on its hangers). And yes, he did develop a basic skincare routine of cleansing and moisturizing (though anything beyond that still made him squirm). But at his core, he was still my sweet, easygoing, comfortably rumpled Maxwell.

As Mr. Snuffles so inelegantly put it: “I told you all along the man was happy just being his natural, scruffy self. But you simply had to go sticking your well-meaning snout where it didn’t belong.”

You know what? For once, I can’t even argue with the snarky mutt’s sass-laden barbs. Because at the end of the day, he was absolutely right. My relentless pursuit of “refinement” was really just a misguided attempt to mold Max into some idealized version of boyfriend perfection.

But true perfection, I’ve come to realize, has nothing to do with designer clothes or fabulously coiffed hair or expertly moisturized skin. No, true perfection lies in the quirks, the flaws, the endearing little idiosyncrasies that make someone uniquely, unapologetically them.

For Max, that meant rocking his signature tousled bedhead and slightly fraying graphic tees. It meant feeling most himself in a worn pair of jeans, not a sleek suit from the menswear department. And it meant accepting his boyfriend just the way he was – a lovable, low-maintenance goofball who didn’t need any grand makeover to be wonderful in my eyes.

So while this particular training endeavor may have been rife with chaos, mishaps, and way too many up-close encounters with potent skincare products, it ultimately taught me a valuable lesson: The secret to true happiness in a relationship isn’t about changing your partner or forcing them into your vision of perfection. It’s about celebrating the unique bundle of quirks and qualities that make them who they are – cozy imperfections, adorable flaws, and all.

“You mean to tell me that after all the grooming trauma you just put that poor guy through, the big lesson here is to love him for his innate doggish ways?” Mr. Snuffles arches one fuzzy eyebrow at me over the rim of his cigar. “Well, bravo Penelope. It only took an exploded facial routine and a disastrous haircut to learn that simple truth.”

I can’t even be mad at his sarcastic jibes this time, though. Not when Max chooses that very moment to wander in, his shaggy hair gloriously tousled and his soft old t-shirt hanging perfectly rumpled from our earlier cuddle session on the couch.

“There’s my ruggedly handsome boyfriend,” I sigh contentedly, pulling him in for a warm embrace and burying my face in the comforting, familiar scent of his worn cotton tee.

Max just chuckles and drops a kiss on the top of my head. “You know you wouldn’t have me any other way, Pen.”

He’s absolutely right.

This is close to the final chapter, but not entirely because I edited it. However, I thought the writing was good enough that the edits were minimal. There was a lot of megaprompting, including scene brief and writing style, that went into the AI, but overall, I like Sonnet’s voice and ability to “create.”

End of Excerpt: to read more please find Sit, Stay, Heel: Training Your Boyfriend Like a Pro at https://books2read.com/sitstayheel ⁠1

ACKNOWLEDGMENTS

I’m grateful for Elizabeth Ann West’s generosity in teaching and sharing her knowledge and brainstorms on using AI for writing. I started with her first Gumroad class and followed her through her YouTube channel and Future Fiction Academy.

Elizabeth’s vision is unparalleled in developing workflows, methods, and experiments. She is definitely a pioneer of AI writing and an advocate for indie authors, representing us with the big foundational models in their developer forums.

I’m profoundly grateful to Stephanie Pajonas for her pivotal role in creating a vibrant community of AI enthusiasts. Her two Facebook groups, AI Writing for Authors and AI Art for Authors have provided a safe and encouraging space for writers to explore this new technology. Stephanie’s advocacy for inclusivity, particularly in amplifying the voices of marginalized writers, is truly commendable.

The Future Fiction Academy is a welcoming and energetic group of authors who are supportive of AI and eagerly share their findings. I’m thankful that Elizabeth, Steph, and Leeland took time away from their writing careers to create this guild, community, university, and hangout spot for authors.

Finally, I’m encouraged by my Romance In A Month writing group and the individual members. We all have a common goal, to write the best romances that we can. Now that we’re aware of AI, I’m encouraged by their open minds and support. Even though the group was not started as an AI writing group, no one in the group gave me grief about introducing AI to the group. It just shows that the people who joined, whether in 2013 or 2024, are open-minded and respectful—happy to help and affirm the life lessons we all learn on this romantic journey we share.

I’m also thankful for you, dear reader, as each one of you is a pioneer. There is no “one way” to do things with AI, which is always changing and hard to keep up with. I’m eager to hear your experiences and discoveries. Happy trails!

ABOUT THE AUTHOR - WRITTEN BY GEMINI 1.5 PRO

Rachelle Ayala’s Romance and Fiction Writing:

Romance Writing:

Prolific and Diverse: Rachelle Ayala has authored a wide range of romance novels, spanning various subgenres such as contemporary romance, paranormal romance, romantic suspense, and historical romance.

Focus on Relationships and Emotional Journeys: Her romance novels often delve into the complexities of relationships, exploring themes of love, loss, forgiveness, and personal growth.

Strong Female Characters: Ayala’s heroines are typically strong, independent women who face challenges and overcome obstacles with determination and resilience.

Compelling Love Interests: Her male protagonists are often charming, supportive, and protective, offering a balance of strength and vulnerability.

Emotional Depth and Engaging Plots: Ayala’s romance novels are known for their emotional depth, engaging plotlines, and satisfying resolutions that leave readers with a sense of hope and happiness.

Fiction Writing (Beyond Romance):

Genre-Blending and Experimentation: Ayala’s fiction writing extends beyond the romance genre, exploring elements of fantasy, science fiction, and mystery. She often blends genres to create unique and captivating narratives.

Fast-Paced and Action-Packed: Her fiction often features fast-paced plots, exciting action sequences, and unexpected twists and turns that keep readers on the edge of their seats.

Diverse Cast of Characters: Ayala’s fiction features a diverse range of characters with unique personalities, backgrounds, and motivations.

Themes of Hope and Resilience: Despite the challenges and conflicts faced by her characters, Ayala’s stories often convey themes of hope, resilience, and the power of the human spirit.

Style and Tone:

Clear and Engaging Prose: Ayala’s writing style is clear, concise, and engaging, making her stories accessible to a wide range of readers.

Vivid Descriptions: She uses vivid imagery and sensory details to bring her settings and characters to life.

Emotional Depth: Ayala’s writing evokes a wide range of emotions in readers, from joy and laughter to sadness and suspense.

Impact and Influence:

Rachelle Ayala’s extensive body of work has established her as a successful and versatile author within the romance and fiction genres. Her willingness to embrace new technologies, such as AI-assisted writing, has positioned her as a pioneer in the evolving landscape of storytelling. Her books and insights continue to inspire and empower writers around the world.

It’s important to note that this analysis is based on a limited sample of Rachelle Ayala’s work and may not encompass the full breadth and depth of her writing style and themes.

MEET RACHELLE

Rachelle Ayala is a USA Today bestselling author of dramatic romantic suspense and humorous contemporary romances. She is the winner of multiple awards, including the 2015 Angie Ovation Award for best Multicultural Romance with Knowing Vera, the 2015 Readers’ Favorite Gold Award for A Father for Christmas, the 2016 Readers’ Favorite Gold Award for Christmas Stray, the 2016 Readers’ Favorite Finalist for A Pet for Christmas, and the 2017 Readers’ Favorite Gold Award for Playing for the Save.

She is also a nonfiction author of writing books and founder of the Romance In A Month method.

WRITING BOOKS

Romance In A Month: Guide to Writing a Romance in 30 Days - Textbook for Romance In A Month method. Includes class slides, character and plot development exercises, list of tropes, first-date ideas, title ideas, and more.

366 Ways To Know Your Character: A Romance In A Month Daily Writing Workbook - Daily character development questions. Useful for getting to know your characters and for brainstorming.

Love Stories: Writing a Romance Novella in Thirty Days or Less – How to write an effective and engaging romance novella in a few short weeks.

Writing Asian Romance Characters – Guidebook for writing Asian romantic characters: covering history, culture, stereotypes, harmful tropes, and multicultural romance.

Dangerous Love: Writing Romantic Suspense – How to write thrilling romantic suspense novels. Includes eight popular plot types, how to pants and write a series, and more!

Love by the Prompt: A Romance Writer’s Guide to AI-Powered Writing - Harnessing the power of Artificial Intelligence to write imaginative and unique romances quickly and easily.

Write With AI: Guide for Fiction and Nonfiction Authors - Revolutionize storytelling, overcome writer’s block, and thrive in the AI-driven literary world.

An AI Author’s Journal: From 0 to 70000 in 14 Days - Under a tight deadline, see how one bestselling author leveraged AI to craft a 70,000-word novel in just 14 days.

Here’s more about my new pen name, Clare Chu.

My first series is called Misguided Guides, a set of dubious self-help guidebooks for the absurd situations you might find in life or otherwise. The first book, “Why Your Cat Is Plotting to Kill You: A Paranoid Pet Owner’s Manual” is FREE, and the audiobook, too, at a certain online store—see the universal link.

I aim to provide you with many more funny moments as we explore the boundaries of mythology, technology, and humor along with a zany cast of unforgettable and unreliable narrators.
